# General Information | goodPayments.io

This section explains how to integrate with the goodPayments API and is intended for developers looking to automate the payment acceptance process.

goodPayments provides a REST API and uses JSON as the data format. All requests are made via secure HTTPS. The documentation covers all interaction methods in detail – request/response structures, authentication rules, error codes, and recommended integration practices.

### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/api-reference/general-information#core-api-capabilities)

Core API Capabilities

**Request Authentication:** How to obtain and use your API key, authentication rules, and required headers.

**User Information:** Retrieve account details and current merchant balance.

**Invoice Management:** Create new invoices, fetch details for a specific invoice, retrieve a list of all invoices, and cancel active invoices.

**Conversion Rates:** Get up-to-date TRX/USDT exchange rates for payment calculations.

[PreviousReferral Programchevron-left](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/referral-program)
[NextGetting an API Keychevron-right](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/api-reference/getting-an-api-key)

Last updated 1 month ago

# Mass Payouts | goodPayments.io

The **«Mass Payouts»** section is designed for sending bulk payouts in **TRX** or **USDT TRC-20** to multiple addresses simultaneously. The feature is available in the merchant dashboard and allows mass payouts to be processed in three steps: input data, preview, confirmation and processing.

### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/mass-payouts#step-1.-input-data)

Step 1. Input Data

In the first step, the merchant must select the payout currency and provide a recipients list with wallet addresses and payout amounts.

![](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1447951587-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FVCQjYw1NLDjPn5X3vSVm%252Fuploads%252FrtGAJk8aPsh0Yb8J1eKr%252F%25D0%25A1%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B8%25D0%25BC%25D0%25BE%25D0%25BA%2520%25D1%258D%25D0%25BA%25D1%2580%25D0%25B0%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B0%25202026-04-16%2520%25D0%25B2%252016.50.31.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D620829fb-d3ee-4124-b625-aa56d15d85dd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=342402de&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/mass-payouts#currency)

**Currency**

The following currencies are available for mass payouts:

*   **TRX**
    
*   **USDT TRC-20**
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/mass-payouts#recipients-list)

**Recipients List**

Recipients can be added in two ways.

**Manually** – to add a row, click **«+ Add recipient»**, then enter the recipient wallet address and payout amount. To remove all entries, click **«Clear»**.

**File upload** – to upload a file with the recipients list, click **«Upload file»**.

circle-info

Supported file formats: **XLSX**, **CSV**, **TXT**. Maximum file size – **5 MB**.

#### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/mass-payouts#file-format-requirements)

**File Format Requirements**

Each row in the file must contain only two values: wallet address and amount.

**CSV and TXT**

One row = one payout. Use comma as delimiter only:

Format: `address,amount` (no spaces and no extra columns).

**XLSX**

Use the first two columns:

*   **A** – wallet address
    
*   **B** – amount
    

The first row can be a header: `address`.

circle-info

**Check before upload:**

*   the address has no extra characters or spaces;
    
*   the amount must be greater than 0;
    
*   use a dot for decimal values (for example, `1.25`);
    
*   empty rows are removed.
    

Once the recipients list is complete, click **«Continue»**.

### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/mass-payouts#step-2.-preview)

Step 2. Preview

This step displays a summary of the upcoming mass payout:

Parameter

Description

**Transactions**

Total number of recipients in the payout

**Total payout**

Total amount of funds to be sent

**goodPayments fee**

Service fee in TRX for processing the mass payout

**Activation cost**

Cost of activating new addresses in TRX (if applicable)

![](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1447951587-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FVCQjYw1NLDjPn5X3vSVm%252Fuploads%252FFEziJes0dxm2w2Hnbn8w%252F%25D0%25A1%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B8%25D0%25BC%25D0%25BE%25D0%25BA%2520%25D1%258D%25D0%25BA%25D1%2580%25D0%25B0%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B0%25202026-04-16%2520%25D0%25B2%252016.51.21.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D41fd00ea-4fd1-404e-8eff-c490c28e3350&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bfdc6595&sv=2)

To proceed, click **«Continue»**. To return to editing the recipients list, click **«Back»**.

### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/mass-payouts#step-3.-confirmation-and-processing)

Step 3. Confirmation and Processing

In the third step, goodPayments generates a **temporary payout address** to which the merchant must transfer the required amount.

![](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1447951587-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FVCQjYw1NLDjPn5X3vSVm%252Fuploads%252F3umWSCcm1g4HNQAQtKcu%252F%25D0%25A1%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B8%25D0%25BC%25D0%25BE%25D0%25BA%2520%25D1%258D%25D0%25BA%25D1%2580%25D0%25B0%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B0%25202026-04-16%2520%25D0%25B2%252016.51.34.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1c05728c-b252-4ddd-b9d1-e6aea07e2603&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=42b48132&sv=2)

The following information is displayed at this step:

*   **Temporary payout address** – the address to top up, with a copy button and a QR code for scanning;
    
*   **Required top-up** – the exact amount in USDT to be sent to the temporary address;
    
*   **Status** – the current state of the mass payout;
    
*   **Progress** – a counter in the format `Sent: X, Failed: X, Pending: X`.
    

Once funds are received at the temporary payout address, the service will automatically initiate payouts to all specified addresses. The progress bar will reflect the processing status in real time.

circle-exclamation

If there are insufficient funds on the payout address, the service will display a corresponding notification indicating the amount still required.

Once the payout is complete, click **«New mass payout»** to start a new one.

### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/mass-payouts#payout-history)

Payout History

All mass payouts are recorded in the **«Invoices»** section – the full history of all payments and transactions.

To filter the table by mass payouts only, look for records with the address type **«Mailings»** displayed in the corresponding column.

Clicking on an **invoice ID** opens a page with detailed information about the payout:

*   current invoice status and expiry details;
    
*   expected and actually received amounts;
    
*   to view data on each individual payout transaction, click **«View transactions»**.
    

[PreviousAML Checkschevron-left](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/aml-checks)
[NextReferral Programchevron-right](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/referral-program)

Last updated 5 days ago

*   [Step 1. Input Data](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/mass-payouts#step-1.-input-data)
    
*   [Step 2. Preview](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/mass-payouts#step-2.-preview)
    
*   [Step 3. Confirmation and Processing](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/mass-payouts#step-3.-confirmation-and-processing)
    
*   [Payout History](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/mass-payouts#payout-history)

# Invoice Creation | goodPayments.io

The **«Invoices»** section of the merchant dashboard is designed for managing payment requests issued to customers. In this section, the merchant can create new invoices and track the full transaction history of all payments.

### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/invoice-creation#creating-an-invoice)

**Creating an Invoice**

To create an invoice, click the **«New Invoice»** button. A modal window will appear with the invoice creation form.

The first step is to select the address type:

*   **Temporary address** – a one-time address that remains active for a defined period (30 minutes by default). Suitable for one-off payments.
    
*   **Static address** – a permanent address that can receive multiple incoming payments and stays active until manually deactivated by the merchant.
    

The set of available fields and the address logic differ depending on the selected address type.

#### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/invoice-creation#temporary-address)

Temporary address

![](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1447951587-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FVCQjYw1NLDjPn5X3vSVm%252Fuploads%252FpEHpp1vkunL9hhiCHYyt%252F%25D0%25A1%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B8%25D0%25BC%25D0%25BE%25D0%25BA%2520%25D1%258D%25D0%25BA%25D1%2580%25D0%25B0%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B0%25202026-04-17%2520%25D0%25B2%252011.19.49.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd8694d1-0deb-4ae7-9580-4cc5232f5ae6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=92d30983&sv=2)

The modal contains the following fields for the merchant to fill out:

Field

Required

Description

**Amount USDT**

Required

The amount to be paid for this invoice (in USD/USDT).

**Include fees in the invoice amount**

Optional

The fee forwarding flag adds the service fee to the invoice amount.

If this option is active, the service fee is added to the invoice total and is paid by the buyer.

**Allowed Currencies**

Required

Selector of allowed payment currencies. Options: • TRX • USDT (TRC-20) • TRX and USDT (TRC-20): both tokens are accepted.

**Expiry (minutes)**

Optional

The duration for which the invoice remains active. Default is **30 minutes**.

**Order ID**

Optional

The order identifier in the merchant's system.

**Redirect URL**

Optional

URL to which the payer will be redirected after completing the payment.

**Webhook URL**

Optional

URL where goodPayments will send the payment notification once the payer completes the invoice.

**Comment**

Optional

Order description. May include any specific information related to the payment.

After completing all required fields, click **«Create»**. The newly created invoice will appear in the payment history table in the **«Invoices»** section.

#### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/invoice-creation#static-address)

Static address

![](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1447951587-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FVCQjYw1NLDjPn5X3vSVm%252Fuploads%252FliEeJEjahsRwgiUfvNBy%252F%25D0%25A1%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B8%25D0%25BC%25D0%25BE%25D0%25BA%2520%25D1%258D%25D0%25BA%25D1%2580%25D0%25B0%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B0%25202026-03-23%2520%25D0%25B2%252014.50.58.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9ec6c55c-bac5-4dd1-a710-c6e6308d65c0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1f301485&sv=2)

A static address is a permanent address for receiving payments that stays active until manually deactivated. Unlike a temporary address, it has no expiration time and can receive an unlimited number of payments.

The modal contains the following fields:

Field

Required

Description

**Allowed Currencies**

Required

Selector of allowed payment currencies. Options: • TRX • USDT (TRC-20) • TRX and USDT (TRC-20): both tokens are accepted.

**Order ID**

Optional

The order identifier in the merchant's system.

**Webhook URL**

Optional

URL where goodPayments will send the payment notification once the payer completes the invoice.

**Comment**

Optional

Order description. May include any specific information related to the payment.

The **Expiry (minutes)** field is not available for static addresses – invoices of this type have no expiration time.

circle-info

The payment window link for a static address never expires and does not display a countdown timer. The link becomes inactive only after the merchant deactivates the address.

**Deactivating a static address** – to stop accepting payments on a static address, the address must be deactivated. This is done using the **«Cancel»** button located in the **«Actions»** column of the invoices table.

### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/invoice-creation#payment-history)

**Payment History**

The payment history is displayed as a table containing records of all invoices created by the merchant.

The table includes the following columns:

*   **Invoice ID** – unique identifier of the invoice. Clicking the ID opens the detailed invoice page.
    
*   **Payment Link** – link to the payment window of the invoice, with a **«Copy»** button for convenience.
    
*   **Payment Transaction** – link to the hash of the incoming transaction associated with this invoice.
    
*   **Address** – the address generated for receiving funds from the payer.
    
*   **Address Type** – temporary or static.
    
*   **Time** – date and time when the invoice was created.
    
*   **Payment Currencies** – currencies allowed for payment.
    
*   **Network** – the blockchain network used for receiving funds.
    
*   **Status** – the current status of the invoice.
    
*   **Amount** – the expected payment amount.
    
*   **Actions** – button to cancel the invoice.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/invoice-creation#invoice-details)

**Invoice Details**

After an invoice is created, the merchant can access a detailed invoice page by clicking the invoice ID in the payment history table.

The detailed invoice page contains five main blocks:

#### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/invoice-creation#id-1.-general-information)

**1\. General Information**

Includes:

*   Invoice ID
    
*   Current status
    
*   Date and time of creation
    
*   Expiration date and time
    
*   Date and time of the last status update
    
*   Link to the transaction hash of the temporary address activation
    
*   Link to the payment window
    
*   Address type
    
*   Order ID in the merchant's system
    
*   Allowed payment currencies
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/invoice-creation#id-2.-amounts)

**2\. Amounts**

Displays the requested and actual amounts:

*   Expected payment amount
    
*   Amount received
    
*   Amount forwarded to the merchant
    
*   Invoice comment (if none was provided, displays “No comment”)
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/invoice-creation#id-3.-transactions)

**3\. Transactions**

Contains blockchain data on both receiving and forwarding operations:

*   Link to the transaction hash of the incoming payment
    
*   Link to the transaction hash of the forwarded payment
    
*   Receiving addresses – the payer’s address and the temporary address generated for the invoice
    
*   Forwarding addresses – the temporary invoice address and the merchant’s payout address
    

For static addresses, transactions are displayed in a modal window accessible by clicking the **«View Transactions»** button. The modal includes additional data:

*   Amount received per transaction
    
*   Payment currency
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/invoice-creation#id-4.-redirects-and-webhooks)

**4\. Redirects and Webhooks**

Includes URLs:

*   Redirect URL where the payer is sent after completing the payment
    
*   Webhook URL where goodPayments sends the payment notification
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/invoice-creation#id-5.-aml-check)

**5\. AML Check**

When the AML checks feature is enabled, an additional AML block is displayed. Clicking the **«View AML Checks»** button redirects the merchant to the **«AML»** section of the dashboard.

[PreviousBalance Top-Upchevron-left](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/balance-top-up)
[NextPayment Windowchevron-right](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/payment-window)

Last updated 5 days ago

*   [Creating an Invoice](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/invoice-creation#creating-an-invoice)
    
*   [Payment History](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/invoice-creation#payment-history)
    
*   [Invoice Details](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/user-guide/invoice-creation#invoice-details)

# Ответы на часто задаваемые вопросы | goodPayments.io

chevron-rightЧто такое goodPayments и как он работает?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/documentation/ru/faq/otvety-na-chasto-zadavaemye-voprosy#chto-takoe-goodpayments-i-kak-on-rabotaet)

goodPayments – это сервис, позволяющий вашему бизнесу принимать платежи в криптовалюте. Он генерирует уникальный адрес для оплаты по каждому инвойсу, отслеживает поступление средств и автоматически пересылает их напрямую на кошелек мерчанта без хранения у себя.

chevron-rightНужно ли проходить KYC для использования сервиса?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/documentation/ru/faq/otvety-na-chasto-zadavaemye-voprosy#nuzhno-li-prokhodit-kyc-dlya-ispolzovaniya-servisa)

Нет, регистрация и использование сервиса не требуют прохождения KYC. Пользователь заполняет форму, получает доступ в личный кабинет и добавляет собственный адрес для получения платежей.

chevron-rightКакие сети и криптовалюты поддерживаются?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/documentation/ru/faq/otvety-na-chasto-zadavaemye-voprosy#kakie-seti-i-kriptovalyuty-podderzhivayutsya)

На текущем этапе сервис поддерживает оплату в блокчейне Tron и токенами TRX и USDT (TRC-20). В дальнейшем планируется расширение списка сетей и токенов.

chevron-rightКак создать инвойс?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/documentation/ru/faq/otvety-na-chasto-zadavaemye-voprosy#kak-sozdat-invois)

Инвойс можно создать в личном кабинете или через API. Достаточно указать сумму, разрешенные валюты, срок действия инвойса, комментарий по оплате и при необходимости – URL-адреса для отправки уведомлений (webhook) и перенаправления пользователя после оплаты. После создания инвойса генерируется платежное окно и временный адрес.

chevron-rightЧто такое временный адрес и зачем он нужен?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/documentation/ru/faq/otvety-na-chasto-zadavaemye-voprosy#chto-takoe-vremennyi-adres-i-zachem-on-nuzhen)

Временный адрес – одноразовый адрес, автоматически создаваемый под конкретный инвойс. Он используется только на время действия инвойса для приема оплаты от плательщика и не предназначен для хранения средств.

chevron-rightЧто такое статичный адрес и чем он отличается от временного?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/documentation/ru/faq/otvety-na-chasto-zadavaemye-voprosy#chto-takoe-statichnyi-adres-i-chem-on-otlichaetsya-ot-vremennogo)

Статичный адрес – это постоянный адрес, который остается активном до момента ручной деактивации мерчантом. В отличие от временного адреса, статичный адрес может принимать неограниченное количество входящих платежей.

chevron-rightЧто такое адрес для пересылок и кто его контролирует?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/documentation/ru/faq/otvety-na-chasto-zadavaemye-voprosy#chto-takoe-adres-dlya-peresylok-i-kto-ego-kontroliruet)

Адрес для пересылок – это конечный адрес мерчанта, на который goodPayments автоматически пересылает средства после оплаты. Этот адрес полностью контролируется мерчантом, сервис не имеет к нему доступа.

chevron-rightКак производится активация адресов и почему это вообще нужно?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/documentation/ru/faq/otvety-na-chasto-zadavaemye-voprosy#kak-proizvoditsya-aktivaciya-adresov-i-pochemu-eto-voobshe-nuzhno)

Новые адреса в блокчейне Tron неактивны. Чтобы с них можно было отправлять транзакции, требуется активация через отправку минимально возможного количества TRX (0.000001 TRX). Если по инвойсу поступает TRX – адрес активируется автоматически; если поступает USDT – активация происходит через баланс активаций мерчанта.

chevron-rightКакие комиссии взимает сервис и в чем отличие?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/documentation/ru/faq/otvety-na-chasto-zadavaemye-voprosy#kakie-komissii-vzimaet-servis-i-v-chem-otlichie)

Комиссия за обработку платежа – 6,5 TRX или 13 TRX, в зависимости от того, какой токен отправляется по инвойсу и есть ли USDT на конечном адресе мерчанта.

**6,5 TRX** – оплата по инвойсу совершается в TRX / оплата совершается в USDT и на адресе мерчанта есть USDT;

**13 TRX** – оплата по инвойсу совершается в USDT и на адресе мерчанта USDT нет.

Комиссия не удерживается из суммы платежа, а списывается с баланса мерчанта.

chevron-rightМожно ли включить комиссию сервиса в сумму инвойса?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/documentation/ru/faq/otvety-na-chasto-zadavaemye-voprosy#mozhno-li-vklyuchit-komissiyu-servisa-v-summu-invoisa)

Да. При создании инвойса доступен флаг **«Включить комиссии в сумму инвойса»**. Если он активирован, комиссия сервиса добавляется к сумме к оплате и выставляется плательщику – он платит больше, чем исходная сумма заказа. С баланса мерчанта комиссия при этом списывается в обычном порядке: мерчант возвращает ее за счет средств, включенных в инвойс.

chevron-rightЧто будет, если баланс TRX закончится? Обработка платежей остановится?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/documentation/ru/faq/otvety-na-chasto-zadavaemye-voprosy#chto-budet-esli-balans-trx-zakonchitsya-obrabotka-platezhei-ostanovitsya)

Если на балансе мерчанта недостаточно TRX для покрытия комиссии, сервис приостанавливает обработку платежей и пересылку средств до пополнения баланса. Уже созданные инвойсы могут не обработаться.

chevron-rightЧто произойдет, если плательщик отправит сумму больше, чем указано в инвойсе?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/documentation/ru/faq/otvety-na-chasto-zadavaemye-voprosy#chto-proizoidet-esli-platelshik-otpravit-summu-bolshe-chem-ukazano-v-invoise)

Сервис обрабатывает весь платеж и переводит всю полученную сумму мерчанту, инвойс получает статус **«Переплачен»**. Возврат или компенсация переплаты решается напрямую между плательщиком и мерчантом, сервис в этом не участвует.

chevron-rightЧто будет, если плательщик отправил меньше, чем указано в инвойсе?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/documentation/ru/faq/otvety-na-chasto-zadavaemye-voprosy#chto-budet-esli-platelshik-otpravil-menshe-chem-ukazano-v-invoise)

Сервис обрабатывает поступившую сумму сразу после получения первой транзакции и переводит все полученные средства мерчанту. Инвойс получает статус **«Недоплачен»**. Вопрос компенсации недостающей суммы решается напрямую между плательщиком и мерчантом, сервис в этом не участвует.

chevron-rightЧто делать, если плательщик отправил криптовалюту, отличную от указанной в инвойсе? [hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/documentation/ru/faq/otvety-na-chasto-zadavaemye-voprosy#chto-delat-esli-platelshik-otpravil-kriptovalyutu-otlichnuyu-ot-ukazannoi-v-invoise)

Такой платеж не обрабатывается автоматически, инвойс получает статус «Ошибка», так как сервис не может корректно определить и обработать поступивший токен. Для решения ситуации необходимо обратиться в поддержку.

chevron-rightМожно ли оплатить инвойс другой криптовалютой, если она поддерживается сервисом?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/documentation/ru/faq/otvety-na-chasto-zadavaemye-voprosy#mozhno-li-oplatit-invois-drugoi-kriptovalyutoi-esli-ona-podderzhivaetsya-servisom)

Нет. Даже если токен поддерживается сервисом, оплата должна производиться только в той валюте, которая указана в инвойсе (TRX, USDT или обе, если разрешено). Использование любого другого токена приведет к ошибке.

chevron-rightЧто такое AML проверки и зачем они нужны?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/documentation/ru/faq/otvety-na-chasto-zadavaemye-voprosy#chto-takoe-aml-proverki-i-zachem-oni-nuzhny)

AML (Anti-Money Laundering) – проверка активов (которые поступают в рамках входящих транзакций) на связь с незаконной деятельностью. При включенной функции AML каждый входящий плтаеж анализируется на предмет риска. Управление функцией доступно в личном кабинете мерчанта.

chevron-rightЧто такое массовые рассылки и как ими пользоваться?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/documentation/ru/faq/otvety-na-chasto-zadavaemye-voprosy#chto-takoe-massovye-rassylki-i-kak-imi-polzovatsya)

Массовые рассылки – инструмент для одновременной отправки выплат в TRX или USDT TRC-20 на множество адресов. Список получателей и суммы можно загрузить файлом в формате XLSX, CSV или TXT, либо ввести вручную.

Процесс состоит из трех шагов: ввод данных → предпросмотр → подтверждение. На третьем шаге сервис генерирует временный адрес рассылки – как только на него поступят средства, рассылка запустится автоматически. История рассылок доступна в разделе **«Инвойсы»** по типу адреса **«Рассылок»**.

chevron-rightКак работает реферальная программа?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/documentation/ru/faq/otvety-na-chasto-zadavaemye-voprosy#kak-rabotaet-referalnaya-programma)

Каждому мерчанту доступна персональная реферальная ссылка. При регистрации нового мерчанта по этой ссылке он закрепляется за реферером. С каждого пополнения основного кошелька (баланса пересылок) привлеченного партнера начисляется бонус в размере **5%**. Сумма сразу зачисляется на баланс пересылок реферера и доступна для использования в сервисе.

Пополнения кошелька активаций, оплата инвойсов и прочие операции в расчет не входят.

chevron-rightКуда обращаться при возникновении технических ошибок?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/documentation/ru/faq/otvety-na-chasto-zadavaemye-voprosy#kuda-obrashatsya-pri-vozniknovenii-tekhnicheskikh-oshibok)

По всем вопросам, связанным с работой сервиса вы можете обратиться в поддержку через Telegram: [@goodp\_managerarrow-up-right](https://t.me/goodp_manager)
.

# Frequently Asked Questions | goodPayments.io

chevron-rightWhat is goodPayments and how does it work?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/faq/frequently-asked-questions#what-is-goodpayments-and-how-does-it-work)

goodPayments is a service that enables your business to accept cryptocurrency payments. For each invoice, the system generates a unique payment address, monitors incoming funds in real time, and automatically forwards them directly to the merchant’s wallet – without storing any funds on its side.

chevron-rightDo I need to complete KYC to use the service?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/faq/frequently-asked-questions#do-i-need-to-complete-kyc-to-use-the-service)

No. Registration and use of the service do not require KYC. You simply fill out the registration form, access your dashboard, and add your own payout address.

chevron-rightWhich chains and cryptocurrencies are supported?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/faq/frequently-asked-questions#which-chains-and-cryptocurrencies-are-supported)

At the current stage, goodPayments supports payments on the Tron blockchain using TRX and USDT (TRC-20). Additional networks and tokens will be added over time.

chevron-rightHow do I create an invoice?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/faq/frequently-asked-questions#how-do-i-create-an-invoice)

An invoice can be created either from the merchant dashboard or via API. You specify the amount, allowed payment currencies, invoice expiration time, optional comments, and – if needed – URLs for webhook notifications and post-payment redirects.

Once created, the system generates a payment page and a temporary (one-time) address for receiving funds.

chevron-rightWhat is a temporary address and why is it needed?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/faq/frequently-asked-questions#what-is-a-temporary-address-and-why-is-it-needed)

A temporary address is a one-time blockchain address generated specifically for an invoice. It is active only for the duration of the invoice and is used solely to receive the payment. It is not intended for storing funds.

chevron-rightWhat is a static address and how is it different from a temporary one?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/faq/frequently-asked-questions#what-is-a-static-address-and-how-is-it-different-from-a-temporary-one)

A static address is a permanent address that stays active until manually deactivated by the merchant. Unlike a temporary address, a static address can receive an unlimited number of incoming payments.

chevron-rightWhat is a forwarding address and who controls it?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/faq/frequently-asked-questions#what-is-a-forwarding-address-and-who-controls-it)

The forwarding address is the merchant’s own address where goodPayments automatically forwards the received funds.

This wallet belongs entirely to the merchant – the service has no access or control over it.

chevron-rightHow are addresses activated and why is activation required?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/faq/frequently-asked-questions#how-are-addresses-activated-and-why-is-activation-required)

New Tron addresses are inactive by default. To send transactions from them, they must be activated by sending the minimum amount of TRX (0.000001 TRX).

*   If the payer sends **TRX**, the address is activated automatically.
    
*   If the payer sends **USDT**, the system activates the address using the merchant’s Activation Balance.
    

chevron-rightWhat fees does the service charge?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/faq/frequently-asked-questions#what-fees-does-the-service-charge)

The processing fee is **6.5 TRX** or **13 TRX**, depending on the payment token and whether the merchant’s payout address contains USDT:

*   **6.5 TRX** – payment made in TRX OR payment made in USDT and the merchant’s payout address already holds USDT
    
*   **13 TRX** – payment made in USDT and the merchant’s payout address does not hold USDT
    

The fee is **not deducted from the payment amount** – it is charged from the merchant’s TRX balance.

chevron-rightCan the service fee be included in the invoice amount?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/faq/frequently-asked-questions#can-the-service-fee-be-included-in-the-invoice-amount)

Yes. When creating an invoice, the **«Include fees in the invoice amount»** flag is available. If enabled, the service fee is added to the invoice total and paid by the payer – they pay more than the original order amount. The fee is still debited from the merchant's forwarding balance as usual: the merchant recovers it through the amount included in the invoice.

chevron-rightWhat happens if the TRX balance runs out?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/faq/frequently-asked-questions#what-happens-if-the-trx-balance-runs-out)

If the merchant does not have enough TRX to cover processing fees, payment handling is paused until the balance is topped up.

Existing invoices may fail to process until sufficient balance is restored.

chevron-rightWhat happens if the payer sends more than the invoice amount?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/faq/frequently-asked-questions#what-happens-if-the-payer-sends-more-than-the-invoice-amount)

The service processes the entire payment and forwards **the full amount** to the merchant. The invoice is marked as **Overpaid**.

Refunds or compensation for overpayments must be handled directly between the payer and the merchant – the service does not split or return excess amounts.

chevron-rightWhat if the payer sends less than required?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/faq/frequently-asked-questions#what-if-the-payer-sends-less-than-required)

The service processes the received amount immediately upon the first incoming transaction and forwards all received funds to the merchant in full. The invoice is marked as **Underpaid**. Any compensation for the shortfall must be handled directly between the payer and the merchant – the service does not participate in this process.

chevron-rightWhat if the payer sends a different cryptocurrency than specified in the invoice?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/faq/frequently-asked-questions#what-if-the-payer-sends-a-different-cryptocurrency-than-specified-in-the-invoice)

Such payments cannot be processed. The invoice will be marked as **Error**, since the system cannot reliably identify or handle the unexpected token. Support is required to resolve the issue.

chevron-rightCan a payer use another supported token to pay the invoice?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/faq/frequently-asked-questions#can-a-payer-use-another-supported-token-to-pay-the-invoice)

No. Even if the token is supported by the service, the payer must use **only the currencies allowed for that specific invoice** (TRX, USDT, or both). Sending any other token results in an error.

chevron-rightWhat are AML checks and why are they needed?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/faq/frequently-asked-questions#what-are-aml-checks-and-why-are-they-needed)

AML (Anti-Money Laundering) is a screening of assets received in incoming transactions for links to illegal activity. When the AML feature is enabled, every incoming payment is analyzed for risk. The feature can be managed in the merchant dashboard.

chevron-rightWhat are Mass Payouts and how do they work?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/faq/frequently-asked-questions#what-are-mass-payouts-and-how-do-they-work)

Mass Payouts is a tool for sending bulk payments in TRX or USDT TRC-20 to multiple addresses simultaneously. The recipients list and amounts can be uploaded as an XLSX, CSV, or TXT file, or entered manually.

The process consists of three steps: input data → preview → confirmation. On the third step, the service generates a temporary payout address – once funds are received, payouts start automatically. The history of all mass payouts is available in the **«Invoices»** section, filtered by address type **«Mailings»**.

chevron-rightHow does the Referral Program work?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/faq/frequently-asked-questions#how-does-the-referral-program-work)

Every merchant has access to a personal referral link. When a new merchant registers through that link, they are attributed to the referrer. A bonus of **5%** is credited for every top-up of the referred merchant's main (forwarding) wallet. The amount is applied immediately to the referrer's forwarding balance and is available for use in the service.

Activation-wallet top-ups, invoice payments, and other operations do not count toward the bonus.

chevron-rightWhere can I get help with technical issues?[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/faq/frequently-asked-questions#where-can-i-get-help-with-technical-issues)

For any questions related to goodPayments, contact our support on Telegram: [**@goodp\_manager**arrow-up-right](https://t.me/goodp_manager)
.

[PreviousWebhookschevron-left](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/api-reference/webhooks)
[NextContact Uschevron-right](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/additional-info/contact-us)

# Getting an API Key | goodPayments.io

To work with the goodPayments API, you need to obtain a unique personal API key. This key is used to identify your merchant account, authorize requests, and protect your integration from unauthorized access. Please note that an API key is available only to users who have successfully registered in the goodPayments platform.

### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/api-reference/getting-an-api-key#ip-whitelist)

**IP Whitelist**

Before accessing the API key, the merchant must add at least one IP address to the whitelist. API access will only be permitted from the specified addresses.

To add an IP address, go to the **«API»** section in your Dashboard, enter the IP address in IPv4 format in the corresponding field, and click **«Add»**.

circle-info

The maximum number of IP addresses in the whitelist is **5**. If only one address remains in the list, it cannot be deleted.

circle-exclamation

The **«Show Key»** and **«Update Key»** buttons are unavailable until at least one IP address has been added to the whitelist.

### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/api-reference/getting-an-api-key#how-to-get-your-api-key)

**How to get your API key**

1

Go to the **«API»** section in your Dashboard

2

Add at least one IP address to the whitelist

3

Click **«Show key»**

![](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1447951587-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FVCQjYw1NLDjPn5X3vSVm%252Fuploads%252FjTyWYBdSbdqyvxgxAya3%252F%25D0%25A1%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B8%25D0%25BC%25D0%25BE%25D0%25BA%2520%25D1%258D%25D0%25BA%25D1%2580%25D0%25B0%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B0%25202026-04-16%2520%25D0%25B2%252017.51.48.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbf575b0a-6fa0-4442-a01b-087db0cba8ef&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a1f855b&sv=2)

Your API key will appear in a modal window. We strongly recommend storing it securely and never sharing it with third parties.

If needed, you can rotate your API key at any time. To do this, click **«Update key»** – a new API key will be generated after you confirm the action.

[PreviousGeneral Informationchevron-left](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/api-reference/general-information)
[NextAuthentication Processchevron-right](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/api-reference/authentication-process)

Last updated 6 days ago

*   [IP Whitelist](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/api-reference/getting-an-api-key#ip-whitelist)
    
*   [How to get your API key](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/api-reference/getting-an-api-key#how-to-get-your-api-key)

# Get Current Conversion Rate | goodPayments.io

Request to retrieve the current conversion rate. You can specify one of the following values: TRX or USDT.

To perform the request, the `currency` parameter must be passed directly in the URL endpoint.

GET [https://app.goodpayments.io/v1/api/rates?currency=TRXarrow-up-right](https://app.goodpayments.io/v1/api/rates?currency=TRX)

###

Name

Type

Description

Example

Authorization\*

string

Unique Merchant API Key

**Request Body**

This request does not require any parameters in the request body. All necessary parameters are included in the URL endpoint.

If the request does not contain a valid API key in the header or IP address is not in Whitelist, the server will return a **403** response.

If an invalid token is specified in the request, the server returns a **404** response.

Flag that determines who pays the forwarding fee. Only for `SINGLE` invoice type.

true / false

# Get List of Invoices | goodPayments.io

Request for retrieving the list of merchant invoices with support for filtering, pagination, and sorting.

_**Filtering**_

`type` – filter by invoice type (`SINGLE`, `MULTIPLE`, `MULTIPLE_TRANSFER`)

`status` – filter by invoice status (`ACTIVE`, `COMPLETED`, `CANCELED`, `TIMEOUT`, `ERROR`, `AML_FAILED`, `OVERPAID`, `UNDERPAID`)

`currency` – filter by currency (`"TRX"`, `"USDT"`, `"TRX,USDT"`)

`date_from` – return invoices created on or after the specified date (inclusive). Format: `YYYY-MM-DD`

`date_to` – return invoices created on or before the specified date (inclusive). Format: `YYYY-MM-DD`

_**Sorting**_

Use the `ordering` parameter to sort results by `created_at`, `amount`, or `status`.

To sort in descending order, add a `-` prefix, e.g.:

`ordering` = `-created_at`

_**Pagination**_

Controlled by the `limit` and `offset` parameters.

Default `limit`: **10**

Maximum allowed `limit`: **300**

_**Search**_

Search is available by: `id`, `address`, `description`, `status`, `currencies`

GET [https://app.goodpayments.io/v1/api/payment/list?status=TIMEOUT&date\_from=2025-11-21&date\_to=2025-11-24&currency=TRX&ordering=amount&limit=10arrow-up-right](https://app.goodpayments.io/v1/api/payment/list?status=TIMEOUT&date_from=2025-11-21&date_to=2025-11-24&currency=TRX&ordering=amount&limit=10)

### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/api-reference/api-methods-overview-request-response-structure/get-list-of-invoices#headers)

# Get Transaction Information | goodPayments.io

Request to retrieve detailed information about a specific transaction by its hash. If an AML check was performed on the transaction, the response includes an `aml_check` object with the full check results.

GET [https://app.goodpayments.io/v1/api/transaction/{trn\_hash}arrow-up-right](https://app.goodpayments.io/v1/api/transaction/%7Btrn_hash%7D)

This request does not require any parameters in the request body. All necessary parameters are included in the URL endpoint.

# Get List of Transactions | goodPayments.io

Request to retrieve a paginated list of the merchant's transactions with support for filtering, sorting, and search.

_**Filtering**_

`type` – filter by transaction type: (`PAYMENT`, `TRANSFER`, `TOPUP`, `ACTIVATION`)

`invoice_id` – filter by the ID of the associated invoice

`from_address` – filter by sender address

`to_address` – filter by recipient address

`trn_hash` – filter by transaction hash

`has_aml` – filter by AML check presence: (`true`, `false`)

`currency` – filter by currency: (`"TRX"`, `"USDT"`)

`date_from` – return invoices created on or after the specified date (inclusive). Format: `YYYY-MM-DD`

`date_to` – return invoices created on or before the specified date (inclusive). Format: `YYYY-MM-DD`

_**Sorting**_

Use the `ordering` parameter to sort results by `created_at`, `amount`, or `status`.

To sort in descending order, add a `-` prefix, e.g.:

`ordering` = `-created_at`

_**Pagination**_

Controlled by the `limit` and `offset` parameters.

Default `limit`: **10**

_**Search**_

Search is available by: `trn_hash`, `invoice_id`, `type`, `currency`, `from_address`, `to_address`

GET [https://app.goodpayments.io/v1/api/transaction/list?date\_from=2025\_10\_25&has\_aml=truearrow-up-right](https://app.goodpayments.io/v1/api/transaction/list?date_from=2025_10_25&has_aml=true)

### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/api-reference/api-methods-overview-request-response-structure/get-list-of-transactions#headers)

Unique Merchant API Key

94a48138b1f41b9cdb3e12c2ff0c7cbe1c7a5f50a311a5054b903cad84215662

### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/api-reference/api-methods-overview-request-response-structure/get-list-of-transactions#request-body)

**Request Body**

This request does not require any parameters in the request body. All necessary parameters are included in the URL endpoint.

# Create a Mass Payout | goodPayments.io

Request to create a new mass payout (multiple transfer).

POST [https://app.goodpayments.io/v1/api/payment/multiple\_transfer/createarrow-up-right](https://app.goodpayments.io/v1/api/payment/multiple_transfer/create)

### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/api-reference/api-methods-overview-request-response-structure/create-a-mass-payout#headers)

Name

Type

Description

Request Body

Name

Type

Description

Example

target\_wallets\*

object

An object containing a list of addresses and the amount to be sent to each address

currency\*

string

List of accepted tokens. Possible values:

*   `TRX`
    
*   `USDT`
    

USDT

### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/api-reference/api-methods-overview-request-response-structure/create-a-mass-payout#request-example)

**Request** **Example**

Copy

    curl -X 'POST' \
      'https://app.goodpayments.io/v1/api/payment/multiple_transfer/create' \
      -H 'accept: application/json' \
      -H 'Authorization: 94a48138b1f41b9cdb3e12c2ff0c7cbe1c7a5f50a311a5054b903cad84215662' \
      -H 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      -d '{
      "target_wallets": [\
        {\
          "address": "TLpMouAbUvAXTspcXviipKMvijGUczUuGw",\
          "amount": 10\
        },\
        {\
          "address": "TXWGCCTgKMYWXpSSfLzutMMfKgeaCgbfbe",\
          "amount": 35.5\
        }\
      ],
      "currency": "USDT"
    }'

# Cancel an Invoice | goodPayments.io

Request intended to cancel a previously created invoice by its ID. The invoice ID is specified in the URL endpoint.

DELETE [https://app.goodpayments.io/v1/api/payment/{id}/cancelarrow-up-right](https://app.goodpayments.io/v1/api/payment/448255354/cancel)

### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/api-reference/api-methods-overview-request-response-structure/cancel-an-invoice#headers)

Headers

Name

Type

Description

Example

Authorization\*

string

Unique Merchant API Key

94a48138b1f41b9cdb3e12c2ff0c7cbe1c7a5f50a311a5054b903cad84215662

### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/api-reference/api-methods-overview-request-response-structure/cancel-an-invoice#request-body)

**Request Body**

This request does not require any parameters in the request body. All necessary parameters are included in the URL endpoint.

### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/api-reference/api-methods-overview-request-response-structure/cancel-an-invoice#request-example)

**Request** **Example**

Copy

    curl -X 'DELETE' \
      'https://app.goodpayments.io/v1/api/payment/448255354/cancel' \
      -H 'accept: application/json' \
      -H 'Authorization: 94a48138b1f41b9cdb3e12c2ff0c7cbe1c7a5f50a311a5054b903cad84215662'

###

Response Example

200 Success

400 Invoice cannot be canceled

403 Authentication credentials were not provided

404 No Invoice matches the given query

### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/api-reference/api-methods-overview-request-response-structure/cancel-an-invoice#possible-errors)

**Possible Errors**

If the invoice cannot be canceled (for example, the specified invoice is already in the `ERROR`, `TIMEOUT`, `COMPLETED`, or `CANCELLED` status), the server returns a **400** response.

If the request does not contain a valid API key in the header or IP address is not in Whitelist, the server will return a **403** response.

If the request contains an incorrect invoice ID, the server returns a **404** response.

# Create an Invoice | goodPayments.io

Request to create a new invoice (payment request).

POST [https://app.goodpayments.io/v1/api/payment/createarrow-up-right](https://app.goodpayments.io/v1/api/payment/create)

### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/api-reference/api-methods-overview-request-response-structure/create-an-invoice#headers)

Headers

Name

Type

Description

Example

Authorization\*

string

Unique Merchant API Key

94a48138b1f41b9cdb3e12c2ff0c7cbe1c7a5f50a311a5054b903cad84215662

### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/api-reference/api-methods-overview-request-response-structure/create-an-invoice#request-body)

Request Body

Name

Type

Description

Example

type\*

string

Invoice type. `SINGLE` – temporary address; `MULTIPLE` – static address

SINGLE

amount\*

number

Invoice amount in USD

10

currencies\*

string

List of accepted tokens. Possible values:

*   `TRX`
    
*   `USDT`
    
*   `TRX, USDT`
    

\["USDT", "TRX"\]

expiry\_minutes

integer

Time period during which the invoice remains active (in minutes)

30

client\_comission

boolean

Flag that determines who pays the forwarding fee. Only for `SINGLE` invoice type.

*   true – the fee is charged to the client. The invoice amount is increased by the fee, and the client pays the total amount.
    
*   false – the fee is paid by the merchant.
    

true / false

order\_id

string

Order identifier in the merchant's system. Maximum 256 characters

12345

webhook\_url

string

The URL to which goodPayments will send a webhook after the customer completes the payment

https://example.com/webhook

redirect\_url

string

The URL where the customer will be redirected after completing the payment

https://example.com/thank-you

description

string

Order description: may contain any provided information related to the order

Payment for order #123

circle-info

For static addresses (`MULTIPLE`), the fields `amount`, `redirect_url`, and `expiry_minutes` are optional and are ignored.

### 

[hashtag](https://goodpayments.gitbook.io/docs/api-reference/api-methods-overview-request-response-structure/create-an-invoice#request-example)

**Request** **Example**

Copy

    curl -X 'POST' \
      'https://app.goodpayments.io/v1/api/payment/create' \
      -H 'accept: application/json' \
      -H 'Authorization: 94a48138b1f41b9cdb3e12c2ff0c7cbe1c7a5f50a311a5054b903cad84215662' \
      -H 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      -d '{
      "type": "SINGLE",
      "amount": 10,
      "currencies": [\
        "TRX",\
        "USDT"\
      ],
      "expiry_minutes": 30
    }'

# Webhooks | goodPayments.io

Webhooks allow you to automatically receive notifications about invoice status changes without having to constantly poll the API.

Notifications are sent to the URL you specify when creating an invoice – either in your Dashboard or via the API.

To start receiving webhooks, simply include the `webhook_url` parameter when creating an invoice, for example:

Copy

    "webhook_url": "https://example.com/webhook"

Webhooks are triggered whenever the invoice status changes to one of the following:

COMPLETED

The invoice has been paid and the funds have been forwarded to the merchant. For temporary address invoices only.

TIMEOUT

The invoice has expired. For temporary address invoices only.

AML\_FAILED

The payment did not pass the AML check. The funds have been returned to the sender.

OVERPAID

Invoice has been overpaid and funds have been forwarded to the merchant. Temporary address invoices only.

UNDERPAID

Invoice has been underpaid and funds have been forwarded to the merchant. Temporary address invoices only.

ERROR

Invoice was processed with an error.

Static address payment

A payment on a static address invoice has been received and processed. Sent separately for each payment event.

Webhook payload format:

Copy

    {
      "id": 336575574,
      "status": "ACTIVE",
      "type": "SINGLE",
      "paymentURL": "https://app.goodpayments.io/payment/336575574",
      "amount": 10,
      "currencies": [\
        "TRX",\
        "USDT"\
      ],
      "currencies_amounts": {
        "TRX": 33.402357,
        "USDT": 10
      },
      "transfer_amounts": {
        "input": {
          "TRX": 0,
          "USDT": 0
        },
        "output": {
          "TRX": 0,
          "USDT": 0
        }
      },
      "cost": null,
      "client_commission": true,
      "order_id": null,
      "address": "TRWvSiQzhSpLdRAmwDHKtgd7bZb2G2be53",
      "webhook_url": null,
      "redirect_url": null,
      "description": "",
      "merchant_contact": "@username",
      "target_wallets": {},
      "expired_at": "2026-03-17T11:59:07.515594+03:00",
      "created_at": "2026-03-17T11:29:07.518981+03:00"
    }

*   `UNDERPAID`

string

Invoice creation timestamp

2025-11-23T13:58:57.789617+00:00

A webhook is sent only once. If your server does not respond within 10 seconds, the webhook will not be resent. In this case, we recommend checking the invoice status manually via the API whenever needed.
